commit 1209d5ceb3feac2f1782870cecbfda99d9715b37
Author: Geoffrey Corey <coreyg@apache.org>
Date:   Fri Jan 9 11:39:40 2015 -0800

    Add rootbin_asf to tlp-us-*
    
    Adding rootbin_asf will add the svnwcsub-hook under /root/bin/www
    along with the proper perms to allow the svnwcsub daemon to read
    and execute the hook, thereby allowing the same svnwcsub.conf to
    exist between the fbsd hosts and the new puppetized tlp hosts.
    
    It will also allow direct copying of the file from svn and into
    git without having to worry about paths.

commit 12b79630bf17d213d6d16ad3afe94f55c0b5c0f4
Author: Geoffrey Corey <coreyg@apache.org>
Date:   Tue Nov 25 13:34:12 2014 -0800

    Change servername for *.incubator.a.o
    
    It appears that SNI on the AWS host isn't working as expected and
    is using the *.apache.org cert for *.incubator.a.o requests.
    Changing the priority for incubator vhost only reverses the problem.
    
    Forcing the incubator vhost ServerName to be incubator.apache.org
    allows *.incubator.apache.org requests to work properly as well as
    *.apache.org requests. The only downside is that incubator.apache.org
    uses the *.incubator.apache.org cert, and therefore on browsers it will
    not be able to supply site identity information.

 modules/tlp_vhosts/manifests/config.pp     | 2 +-
 modules/tlp_vhosts/manifests/ssl_vhosts.pp | 2 +-
 2 files changed, 2 insertions(+), 2 deletions(-)
